The scripts and functions associated with this work are distributed under the GNU General Public License.
When utilizing this work, please use the following citations for the Downscaling Package and output data:

Mosier, T. M., Hill, D. F., & Sharp, K. V. (2014). 30-Arcsecond monthly 
climate surfaces with global land coverage. International Journal of Climatology,
 34(7), 2175-2188.
Please additionally cite all of the input data sources utilized (e.g. from the Climate Research Unit, Willmott & Matsuura, Global Precipitation Climatology Centre, WorldClim, and/or the Global Historical Climatology Network).
